# Chapter 427: Linked Qi Mechanisms and the Contender of Dao Strife

The usually jovial Hundred Peaks True Lord’s expression turned unusually solemn. "A Dao title is no child's play; it marks the beginning of one's quest for longevity. I once knew a True Lord within the Sacred Sect whose Dao title clashed with his destiny, undoing three hundred years of arduous cultivation in an instant."

Rarely showing such concern, he advised, "Junior Brother, a Dao title concerns your future path of cultivation. It is tied to the threads of destiny in the unseen realms. You must be cautious."

Xu Yunfan naturally understood the implication. A Dao title should neither be too grand nor too humble. If too grand, one cannot bear the weight; if too humble, one cannot ascend. A compromise is necessary.

After a moment of thought, Xu Yunfan spoke.

"Let it be Zhenwu (True Martial)."

The moment the words left Xu Yunfan’s lips, a tempest suddenly erupted within his Purple Mansion. The condensed Divine Martial Dao Base within his body tremble violently.

He clearly sensed a golden chain spanning heaven and earth descending from the void, currently coiling around his Dao Base like a living creature.

*Damn!*

Even with Xu Yunfan’s composure, his expression shifted slightly at this moment. He truly hadn't expected the Dao title "Zhenwu" to bear such a heavy karmic burden. He should have chosen "Shenwu" (Divine Martial) if he had known.

Hundred Peaks True Lord, watching Xu Yunfan’s fluctuating expression, was about to speak when the communication talisman in his sleeve suddenly self-ignited. His expression changed slightly. "True Lord Qingyuan has summoned me for a discussion."

Before leaving in a hurry, he turned back and said, "By the way, the Heavenly Dao of the Divine Martial
